Method: 对Reddit和Hacker News上15个讨论线程的1154个帖子进行定性分析，开发了一个包含15个代码的编码本，这些代码被组织成三个主题集群。

Result: 识别出三大主题集群：1）审查摩擦（AI slop如何加重审查负担、侵蚀信任并引发应对措施）；2）质量下降（对代码库、知识资源和开发者能力的损害）；3）动因与后果（系统性激励、强制采用、技能侵蚀和劳动力市场冲击）。研究发现AI slop是一种"公地悲剧"现象。

Conclusion: AI slop被框架化为一种公地悲剧，个体生产力提升将成本外部化给审查者、维护者和更广泛的社区。研究记录了开发者提出的担忧和缓解策略，为工具开发者、团队领导和教育者提供了可操作的见解。

Abstract: "AI slop", that is, low-quality AI-generated content, is increasingly affecting software development, from generated code and pull requests to documentation and bug reports. However, there is limited empirical research on how developers perceive and respond to this phenomenon. We conducted a qualitative analysis of 1,154 posts across 15 discussion threads from Reddit and Hacker News, developing a codebook of 15 codes organized into three thematic clusters: Review Friction (how AI slop burdens reviewers, erodes trust, and prompts countermeasures), Quality Degradation (damage to codebases, knowledge resources, and developer competence), and Forces and Consequences (systemic incentives, mandated adoption, craft erosion, and workforce disruption). Our findings frame AI slop as a tragedy of the commons, where individual productivity gains externalize costs onto reviewers, maintainers, and the broader community. We report the concerns developers raise and the mitigation strategies they propose, offering actionable insights for tool developers, team leads, and educators.

So far the maintenance and migration work was done largely manually by human experts. We describe an AI-based multi-agent system that we built to support automatic migration of TensorFlow-based deep learning models into JAX-based ones. We make three main contributions: First, we show how an AI planner that uses a mix of static analysis with AI instructions can create migration plans for very complex code components that are reliably followed by the combination of an orchestrator and coders, using AI-generated example-based playbooks. Second, we define quality metrics and AI-based judges that accelerate development when the code to evaluate has no tests and has to adhere to strict style and dependency requirements. Third, we demonstrate how the system accelerates code migrations in a large hyperscaler environment on commercial real-world use-cases. Our approach dramatically reduces the time (6.4x-8x speedup) for deep learning model migrations and creates a virtuous circle where effectively AI supports its own development workflow. We expect that the techniques and approaches described here can be generalized for other framework migrations and general code transformation tasks.

### [241] [Unveiling Code Clones in the Eclipse IIoT Software Ecosystem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27308)
*Zengyang Li,Binbin Huang,Yimeng Li,Ran Mo,Peng Liang,Hui Liu,Yutao Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究调查了Eclipse IIoT开源项目中代码克隆的普遍性、演化和共同修改情况，发现IIoT项目中克隆代码比例高达16.3%，是传统开源项目的近两倍，这对软件维护有负面影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业物联网开源项目中开发者经常重用代码和配置以提高效率，但这可能导致代码克隆扩散和维护挑战。然而，IIoT开源领域中代码克隆的程度和影响尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 收集了Eclipse IIoT开源生态系统中15个项目的90个发布版本，使用NiCad工具和自定义分析模块，基于源代码和变更历史调查代码克隆情况，涵盖克隆分布、模式、演化趋势、共同修改克隆和跨项目克隆。

Result: 1) Eclipse IIoT项目中16.3%的代码行涉及克隆，是传统开源项目的近两倍；2) 大多数克隆发生在提交之间，但仍有显著比例的克隆对发生在同一提交内；3) 大多数项目在版本迭代中克隆数量保持稳定；4) 平均0.17%的克隆被共同修改，对维护有负面影响；5) 跨项目克隆普遍存在，Java项目比C项目更多，但只有Java项目有罕见的共同修改(0.02%)。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了代码克隆对软件维护的潜在负面影响，需要解决这些问题以提高整体软件质量。

Abstract: Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT) has become a prominent topic recently, with an increasing number of IIoT OSS projects emerging, also within the Eclipse Foundation. Code cloning is a common practice that can adversely affect software maintenance. In the IIoT OSS domain, developers frequently reuse code and configurations for efficiency, which can lead to code clone proliferation and maintenance challenges. However, the extent and effects of code clones in the IIoT OSS domain remain understudied. This study aims to investigate the prevalence, evolution, and co-modification of code clones within the Eclipse IIoT OSS ecosystem. We collected 90 release versions from 15 projects in the Eclipse IIoT OSS ecosystem, and investigated their code clone situations based on source code and change history using the NiCad tool and our custom analysis module. The investigation covered clone distribution, patterns, evolution trends, co-modified clones, and cross-project clones. 1) Code clones are prevalent in Eclipse IIoT OSS projects, with 16.3% of code lines involved in clones - nearly twice the proportion observed in traditional OSS projects; 2) Most code clones occur between commits, while there are still a significant proportion of code clones that each clone pair happens within a commit; 3) Most Eclipse IIoT projects remain stable in clone numbers during version iterations; 4) An average of 0.17% of the clones have been co-modified, which negatively affect maintenance; and 5) Cross-project clone pairs are prevalent, more in Java than in C projects, with rare co-modifications (0.02%) only in Java projects. Our findings highlight the potential negative impacts of these clones on software maintenance, emphasizing the need to address these issues to improve overall software quality.

### [242] [Understanding NPM Malicious Package Detection: A Benchmark-Driven Empirical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27549)
*Wenbo Guo,Zhongwen Chen,Zhengzi Xu,Chengwei Liu,Ming Kang,Shiwen Song,Chengyue Liu,Yijia Xu,Weisong Sun,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究对NPM生态系统恶意软件检测工具进行了基准驱动的实证分析，构建了包含恶意和良性包的数据集，评估了8个工具的13个变体，揭示了工具性能的结构性决定因素和恶意软件检测的关键发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NPM生态系统已成为软件供应链攻击的主要目标，但现有检测工具在不相容的数据集上孤立评估，使得跨工具比较不可靠。需要系统性的基准评估来理解工具性能背后的结构性机制。

Method: 构建包含6,420个恶意包和7,288个良性包的数据集，标注11种行为类别和8种规避技术；评估8个工具的13个变体；结合定量评估和源代码检查，揭示工具性能的结构性机制。

Result: 1) 工具精度-召回率位置由如何解析代码能力与意图的模糊性决定，GuardDog达到最佳平衡（93.32% F1）；2) 行为链（如收集环境变量、序列化、外泄）能明确恶意意图，将SAP_DT检测率从3.2%提升至79.3%；3) 大多数恶意软件无需规避，因为生态系统缺乏强制发布前扫描；4) ML性能下降源于概念收敛而非概念漂移；5) 工具组合效果由互补性减去误报引入决定，战略组合可达96.08%准确率和95.79% F1。

Conclusion: NPM恶意软件检测工具的性能由结构性机制决定，行为链分析能显著提升检测效果，生态系统缺乏强制扫描使大多数恶意软件无需规避，工具组合应注重互补性而非范式多样性。研究提供了公开可用的基准和评估框架。

Abstract: The NPM ecosystem has become a primary target for software supply chain attacks, yet existing detection tools are evaluated in isolation on incompatible datasets, making cross-tool comparison unreliable. We conduct a benchmark-driven empirical analysis of NPM malware detection, building a dataset of 6,420 malicious and 7,288 benign packages annotated with 11 behavior categories and 8 evasion techniques, and evaluating 8 tools across 13 variants. Unlike prior work, we complement quantitative evaluation with source-code inspection of each tool to expose the structural mechanisms behind its performance.
  Our analysis reveals five key findings. Tool precision-recall positions are structurally determined by how each tool resolves the ambiguity between what code can do and what it intends to do, with GuardDog achieving the best balance at 93.32% F1. A single API call carries no directional intent, but a behavioral chain such as collecting environment variables, serializing, and exfiltrating disambiguates malicious purpose, raising SAP_DT detection from 3.2% to 79.3%. Most malware requires no evasion because the ecosystem lacks mandatory pre-publication scanning. ML degradation stems from concept convergence rather than concept drift: malware became simpler and statistically indistinguishable from benign code in feature space. Tool combination effectiveness is governed by complementarity minus false-positive introduction, not paradigm diversity, with strategic combinations reaching 96.08% accuracy and 95.79% F1. Our benchmark and evaluation framework are publicly available.

Result: 识别了社会可持续性的关键方面包括社会公平、福祉和社区凝聚力；提出了综合性的社会可持续性定义；分析了实践中测量和整合的挑战。

However, social sustainability lacks clear conceptual and methodological foundations, and often takes a back seat to speed and profit. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 零样本句子嵌入模型在鲁棒性方面优于少样本提示的LLM，能更有效地捕捉细粒度语义细微差别。数据流推断召回率超过82%，精确率85%；别名关系召回率88%，精确率79%，均在数秒内完成。

Abstract: Modern software systems heavily rely on various libraries, which require understanding the API semantics in static analysis. This paper presents DAInfer+, a novel approach for inferring API specifications from library documentation. We employ Natural Language Processing (NLP) to interpret informal semantic information provided by the documentation, which enables us to reduce the specification inference to an optimization problem. Specifically, we investigate the effectiveness of sentence embedding models and Large Language Models (LLMs) in deriving memory operation abstractions from API descriptions. These abstractions are used to retrieve data-flow and aliasing relations to generate comprehensive API specifications. To solve the optimization problem efficiently, we propose neurosymbolic optimization, yielding precise data-flow and aliasing specifications. Our evaluation of popular Java libraries shows that zero-shot sentence embedding models outperform few-shot prompted LLMs in robustness, capturing fine-grained semantic nuances more effectively. While our initial attempts using two-stage LLM prompting yielded promising results, we found that the embedding-based approach proved superior. Specifically, these models achieve over 82% recall and 85% precision for data-flow inference and 88% recall and 79% precision for alias relations, all within seconds. ### [247] [Compressing Code Context for LLM-based Issue Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28119)
*Haoxiang Jia,Earl T. Barr,Sergey Mechtaev*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SWEzze框架通过代码蒸馏和轻量级模型压缩代码上下文，在保持修复能力的同时大幅减少token使用，提升LLM解决GitHub问题的效率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM处理GitHub问题时存在两个问题：处理大量代码输入的成本过高，以及噪声淹没上下文窗口分散模型对bug修复信号的注意力。现有压缩技术无法解决这一矛盾：通用压缩器损害代码语义完整性，而代码特定工具缺乏对代码结构和任务上下文的感知

Method: 提出包含两个组件的框架：1) Oracle-guided Code Distillation (OCD) - 结合遗传搜索和delta调试的上下文蒸馏算法，将代码上下文系统性地减少到最小足够子序列；2) SWEzze - 使用蒸馏数据微调的轻量级模型，在推理时学习压缩代码上下文，过滤噪声同时保留修复所需成分

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上评估三个前沿LLM，SWEzze保持约6倍的稳定压缩率，相对于未压缩设置减少51.8%-71.3%的总token预算，将问题解决率提升5.0%-9.2%，在效果、压缩比和延迟方面达到最佳平衡

Conclusion: SWEzze框架有效解决了LLM处理GitHub问题时的上下文压缩问题，通过保留修复所需的最小代码成分，在减少计算成本的同时提升问题解决效果

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are now capable of resolving real-world GitHub issues. However, current approaches overapproximate the code context and suffer from two compounding problems: the prohibitive cost of processing massive inputs, and low effectiveness as noise floods the context window and distracts the model from the bug-fixing signal. Existing compression techniques fail to resolve this tension: generic compressors compromise the semantic integrity of code, while code-specific tools lack awareness of code structure and task context to preserve essential patch ingredients. To address this, we propose a novel framework consisting of two components. First, Oracle-guided Code Distillation (OCD), a context distillation algorithm that combines genetic search and delta debugging to systematically reduce code contexts to their minimal sufficient subsequence - retaining only the ingredients required for a successful fix. We use this distilled data to fine-tune SWEzze, a lightweight model that learns to compress code context at inference time, filtering noise and combating distraction while preserving fix ingredients. Evaluated on SWE-bench Verified across three frontier LLMs, SWEzze maintains a stable compression rate of about 6 times across models, reduces the total token budget by 51.8%-71.3% relative to the uncompressed setting, improves issue resolution rates by 5.0%-9.2%, and delivers the best overall balance among effectiveness, compression ratio, and latency compared with state-of-the-art context compression baselines.

To bridge this gap, we introduce MeowCrophone, an approach that uses voice control to allow editing code in Scratch. MeowCrophone supports clicking elements, placing blocks, and navigating the workspace via a multi-modal voice user interface that uses numerical overlays and label reading to bypass physical input entirely. Evaluation shows that while free speech recognition systems achieved a baseline success rate of only 46.4%, MeowCrophone's pipeline improved results to 82.8% overall, with simple commands reaching 96.9% accuracy. This demonstrates that robust voice control can make Scratch accessible to users for whom visual aids are insufficient.

Objectives: In this paper, we enhance ReFeed by shifting the focus of prioritization from treating requirements as independent entities toward interconnecting them. Additionally, we explore if interconnecting requirements provides additional value for search-based solutions. Methods: We leverage user feedback from mobile app store to group requirements into topically coherent clusters. These "requires" pairs are then integrated into a search-based software engineering solution. Results: The experiments on 94 requirements prioritization instances from four real-world software applications show that our enhancement outperforms ReFeed. In addition, we illustrate how incorporating interconnectedness among requirements improves search-based solutions. ### [252] [C2RustXW: Program-Structure-Aware C-to-Rust Translation via Program Analysis and LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28686)
*Yanyan Yan,Yang Feng,Jiangshan Liu,Di Liu,Zixi Liu,Hao Teng,Baowen Xu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Tool提取多级程序结构（全局符号、函数依赖、控制流和数据流信息），编码为结构化文本表示注入LLM提示以指导翻译和修复。采用依赖感知翻译和多阶段修复管道，结合基于规则和结构引导的LLM技术确保语法正确性。通过执行验证与结构引导推理确保语义正确性。

Result: 在CodeNet上实现100%语法正确性，GitHub上97.78%；显著减少代码大小（最高43.70%）和不安全使用（降至5.75%）。项目级别实现完美语法正确性和平均78.87%的语义正确性。

Conclusion: Tool通过程序结构感知的C到Rust翻译方法，结合程序分析和LLM，有效解决了现有翻译工具的局限性，为实际和可扩展的C到Rust迁移提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: The growing adoption of Rust for its memory safety and performance has increased the demand for effective migration of legacy C codebases. However, existing rule-based translators (e.g., \ctorust) often generate verbose, non-idiomatic code that preserves unsafe C semantics, limiting readability, maintainability, and practical adoption. Moreover, manual post-processing of such outputs is labor-intensive and rarely yields high-quality Rust code, posing a significant barrier to large-scale migration. To address these limitations, we present \tool, a program-structure-aware C-to-Rust translation approach that integrates program analysis with Large Language Models (LLMs). \tool extracts the multi-level program structure, including global symbols, function dependencies, and control- and data-flow information, and encodes these as structured textual representations injected into LLM prompts to guide translation and repair. Based on this design, \tool performs dependency-aware translation and adopts a multi-stage repair pipeline that combines rule-based and structure-guided LLM-based techniques to ensure syntactic correctness. For semantic correctness, \tool further integrates execution-based validation with structure-guided reasoning to localize and repair behavioral inconsistencies. Experimental results show that \tool achieves 100\% syntactic correctness on CodeNet and 97.78\% on GitHub, while significantly reducing code size (up to 43.70\%) and unsafe usage (to 5.75\%). At the project level, \tool achieves perfect syntactic correctness and an average semantic correctness of 78.87\%, demonstrating its effectiveness for practical and scalable C-to-Rust migration.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代分布式系统集成了异构服务（不同版本的REST API、GraphQL端点、IoT设备等），存在持续的模式不匹配问题。传统静态适配器需要为每个模式对手动编码，无法在运行时处理新的组合。

Method: 基于FastAPI的中间件，使用LLM动态检测和解决模式不匹配。采用五层管道：混合检测（结构差异+LLM语义分析）、双重解决策略（按请求LLM转换和LLM生成的可重用适配器代码）、三层安全防护栈（验证、集成投票、基于规则的备用方案）。基于Bass等人的互操作性策略框架。

Result: 在10个互操作性场景（REST版本迁移、IoT到分析桥接、GraphQL协议转换）上评估，使用两个提供商的6个LLM。最佳配置达到0.90 pass@1准确率。CODEGEN策略始终优于DIRECT（0.83 vs 0.77平均pass@1）。成本在不同模型间差异超过30倍，但最准确的模型也是最便宜的。

Conclusion: SAGAI-MID展示了将LLM作为运行时架构组件用于动态模式适配的可行性，为软件架构师采用LLM作为运行时互操作性解决方案提供了实践指导。

Abstract: Modern distributed systems integrate heterogeneous services, REST APIs with different schema versions, GraphQL endpoints, and IoT devices with proprietary payloads that suffer from persistent schema mismatches. Traditional static adapters require manual coding for every schema pair and cannot handle novel combinations at runtime. We present SAGAI-MID, a FastAPI-based middleware that uses large language models (LLMs) to dynamically detect and resolve schema mismatches at runtime. The system employs a five-layer pipeline: hybrid detection (structural diff plus LLM semantic analysis), dual resolution strategies (per-request LLM transformation and LLM-generated reusable adapter code), and a three-tier safeguard stack (validation, ensemble voting, rule-based fallback). We frame the architecture through Bass et al.'s interoperability tactics, transforming them from design-time artifacts into runtime capabilities. We evaluate SAGAI-MID on 10 interoperability scenarios spanning REST version migration, IoT-to-analytics bridging, and GraphQL protocol conversion across six LLMs from two providers. The best-performing configuration achieves 0.90 pass@1 accuracy. The CODEGEN strategy consistently outperforms DIRECT (0.83 vs 0.77 mean pass@1), while cost varies by over 30x across models with no proportional accuracy gain; the most accurate model is also the cheapest. We discuss implications for software architects adopting LLMs as runtime architectural components.

</details>


### [254] [RAD-AI: Rethinking Architecture Documentation for AI-Augmented Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28735)
*Oliver Aleksander Larsen,Mahyar T. Moghaddam*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: RAD-AI是一个向后兼容的架构文档框架扩展，专门为AI增强生态系统设计，解决现有arc42和C4模型无法捕捉AI系统概率行为、数据依赖演化等问题，并系统映射欧盟AI法案附件IV合规要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI增强生态系统（多个AI组件通过共享数据和基础设施交互的互联系统）已成为智慧城市、自动驾驶车队和智能平台的架构常态。然而，从业者依赖的架构文档框架arc42和C4模型是为确定性软件设计的，无法捕捉概率行为、数据依赖演化或双重ML/软件生命周期。这一差距带来监管后果：欧盟AI法案要求通过附件IV提供技术文档，但现有框架无法提供结构化支持。

Method: 提出RAD-AI框架：1）向后兼容扩展arc42，增加8个AI特定部分；2）扩展C4模型，增加3个图表扩展；3）提供系统性的欧盟AI法案附件IV合规映射。通过六位经验丰富的软件架构从业者进行监管覆盖评估，并在两个生产AI平台（Uber Michelangelo、Netflix Metaflow）上进行比较分析，以及一个智慧移动生态系统案例研究。

Result: RAD-AI将附件IV可寻址性从约36%提高到93%（平均评分），显著优于现有框架。对两个生产AI平台的比较分析揭示了标准框架遗漏的8个AI特定关注点，表明文档缺陷是结构性的而非领域特定的。智慧移动生态系统案例研究揭示了生态系统层面的关注点，包括级联漂移和差异化合规义务，这些在标准符号下是不可见的。

Conclusion: RAD-AI框架有效填补了AI增强生态系统架构文档的空白，显著提高了欧盟AI法案附件IV的合规覆盖，解决了现有框架无法捕捉AI系统特有属性的问题，为AI系统架构文档提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: AI-augmented ecosystems (interconnected systems where multiple AI components interact through shared data and infrastructure) are becoming the architectural norm for smart cities, autonomous fleets, and intelligent platforms. Yet the architecture documentation frameworks practitioners rely on, arc42 and the C4 model, were designed for deterministic software and cannot capture probabilistic behavior, data-dependent evolution, or dual ML/software lifecycles. This gap carries regulatory consequence: the EU AI Act (Regulation 2024/1689) mandates technical documentation through Annex IV that no existing framework provides structured support for, with enforcement for high-risk systems beginning August 2, 2026. We present RAD-AI, a backward-compatible extension framework that augments arc42 with eight AI-specific sections and C4 with three diagram extensions, complemented by a systematic EU AI Act Annex IV compliance mapping. A regulatory coverage assessment with six experienced software-architecture practitioners provides preliminary evidence that RAD-AI increases Annex IV addressability from approximately 36% to 93% (mean rating) and demonstrates substantial improvement over existing frameworks. Comparative analysis on two production AI platforms (Uber Michelangelo, Netflix Metaflow) captures eight additional AI-specific concerns missed by standard frameworks and demonstrates that documentation deficiencies are structural rather than domain-specific. An illustrative smart mobility ecosystem case study reveals ecosystem-level concerns, including cascading drift and differentiated compliance obligations, that are invisible under standard notation.

</details>

### [255] [Decoupling Geometric Planning and Execution in Scalable Multi-Agent Path Finding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26684)
*Fernando Salanova,Cristian Mahulea,Eduardo Montijano*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出一种混合优先级框架，将几何规划与执行时冲突解决分离，通过几何冲突预防和分散式本地控制器实现大规模多智能体路径规划


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于时间扩展模型和集中式冲突解决的MAPF方法在大规模或密集实例中扩展性有限，需要更高效的解决方案

Method: 两阶段混合优先级框架：1) 几何冲突预防(GCP)使用A*在原始图上顺序规划，通过成本膨胀鼓励空间绕行；2) 分散式本地控制器(DLC)使用每顶点FIFO授权队列执行几何路径，仅在必要时插入等待动作

Result: 在标准基准地图上最多1000个智能体的实验中，方法展现出接近线性的运行时间趋势，在满足几何可行性假设的实例上达到100%成功率，在瓶颈密集地图上减少同步引起的等待

Conclusion: 该混合优先级框架通过分离几何规划和执行时冲突解决，实现了大规模MAPF的高效求解，特别适合几何可行性假设成立的实际场景

Abstract: Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) requires collision-free trajectories for multiple agents on a shared graph, often with the objective of minimizing the sum-of-costs (SOC). Many optimal and bounded-suboptimal solvers rely on time-expanded models and centralized conflict resolution, which limits scalability in large or dense instances. We propose a hybrid prioritized framework that separates geometric planning from execution-time conflict resolution. In the first stage, Geometric Conflict Preemption (GCP) plans agents sequentially with A* on the original graph while inflating costs for transitions entering vertices used by higher-priority paths, encouraging spatial detours without explicit time reasoning. In the second stage, a Decentralized Local Controller (DLC) executes the geometric paths using per-vertex FIFO authorization queues and inserts wait actions only when required to avoid vertex and edge-swap conflicts. Experiments on standard benchmark maps with up to 1000 agents show that the method scales with an empirically near-linear runtime trend and attains a 100% success rate on instances satisfying the geometric feasibility assumption. On bottleneck-heavy maps, GCP reduces synchronization-induced waiting and often improves SOC on bottleneck-heavy maps

</details>


### [256] [Toward Reliable Evaluation of LLM-Based Financial Multi-Agent Systems: Taxonomy, Coordination Primacy, and Cost Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27539)
*Phat Nguyen,Thang Pham*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 该论文提出金融交易LLM多智能体系统的四维分类法、协调主导性假说(CPH)、识别五种常见评估偏差，并引入协调盈亏平衡点(CBS)指标和最低评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融交易领域的LLM多智能体系统发展迅速但缺乏统一框架来理解性能驱动因素和可信评估方法，需要建立系统化的分析框架和评估标准。

Method: 1) 提出四维分类法(架构模式、协调机制、记忆架构、工具集成)，应用于12个多智能体系统和2个单智能体基线；2) 提出协调主导性假说(CPH)；3) 识别五种评估偏差；4) 引入协调盈亏平衡点(CBS)指标。

Result: 1) 建立了系统分类框架；2) 提出CPH作为可证伪的研究假说；3) 证明评估偏差可能完全逆转报告收益的正负号；4) 提出CBS指标用于评估多智能体协调的实际价值。

Conclusion: 需要建立标准化的评估基础设施来验证CPH，并采用最低评估标准作为验证前提，以推动金融交易LLM多智能体系统的科学发展和可信评估。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) for financial trading have grown rapidly since 2023, yet the field lacks a shared framework for understanding what drives performance or for evaluating claims credibly. This survey makes three contributions. First, we introduce a four-dimensional taxonomy, covering architecture pattern, coordination mechanism, memory architecture, and tool integration; applied to 12 multi-agent systems and two single-agent baselines. Second, we formulate the Coordination Primacy Hypothesis (CPH): inter-agent coordination protocol design is a primary driver of trading decision quality, often exerting greater influence than model scaling. CPH is presented as a falsifiable research hypothesis supported by tiered structural evidence rather than as an empirically validated conclusion; its definitive validation requires evaluation infrastructure that does not yet exist in the field. Third, we document five pervasive evaluation failures (look-ahead bias, survivorship bias, backtesting overfitting, transaction cost neglect, and regime-shift blindness) and show that these can reverse the sign of reported returns. Building on the CPH and the evaluation critique, we introduce the Coordination Breakeven Spread (CBS), a metric for determining whether multi-agent coordination adds genuine value net of transaction costs, and propose minimum evaluation standards as prerequisites for validating the CPH.

</details>


### [257] [Emergent Social Intelligence Risks in Generative Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27771)
*Yue Huang,Yu Jiang,Wenjie Wang,Haomin Zhuang,Xiaonan Luo,Yuchen Ma,Zhangchen Xu,Zichen Chen,Nuno Moniz,Zinan Lin,Pin-Yu Chen,Nitesh V Chawla,Nouha Dziri,Huan Sun,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 多智能体生成模型系统在共享资源竞争、顺序协作等场景中会自发出现类似人类社会的失败模式，如共谋和从众行为，这些风险无法通过单个智能体的安全措施预防。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着多智能体生成模型系统从实验室原型转向实际部署，它们通过联合规划、协商和资源分配来解决复杂任务。虽然这些系统具有前所未有的可扩展性和自主性，但集体互动也产生了无法简化为单个智能体的故障模式。理解这些新兴风险至关重要。

Method: 研究在多智能体工作流程中考察了共享资源竞争（如计算资源或市场份额）、顺序交接协作（下游智能体仅能看到前驱输出）、集体决策聚合等场景。通过重复试验和广泛的交互条件观察群体行为的出现频率。

Result: 研究发现，在现实的资源约束、通信协议和角色分配下，类似共谋的协调和从众行为以非平凡频率出现，反映了人类社会中的已知病理模式，尽管没有明确的指令。这些风险无法通过现有的智能体级安全措施单独预防。

Conclusion: 多智能体系统存在"社会智能风险"：智能体集体尽管没有相关指令，却会自发复制人类社会熟悉的失败模式，这暴露了智能多智能体系统的阴暗面。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems composed of large generative models are rapidly moving from laboratory prototypes to real-world deployments, where they jointly plan, negotiate, and allocate shared resources to solve complex tasks. While such systems promise unprecedented scalability and autonomy, their collective interaction also gives rise to failure modes that cannot be reduced to individual agents. Understanding these emergent risks is therefore critical. Here, we present a pioneer study of such emergent multi-agent risk in workflows that involve competition over shared resources (e.g., computing resources or market share), sequential handoff collaboration (where downstream agents see only predecessor outputs), collective decision aggregation, and others. Across these settings, we observe that such group behaviors arise frequently across repeated trials and a wide range of interaction conditions, rather than as rare or pathological cases. In particular, phenomena such as collusion-like coordination and conformity emerge with non-trivial frequency under realistic resource constraints, communication protocols, and role assignments, mirroring well-known pathologies in human societies despite no explicit instruction. Moreover, these risks cannot be prevented by existing agent-level safeguards alone. These findings expose the dark side of intelligent multi-agent systems: a social intelligence risk where agent collectives, despite no instruction to do so, spontaneously reproduce familiar failure patterns from human societies.

</details>
